DETECTOR   (TELES,SOLST,GELI) A Solid State Three-Detector        O029100100043 
            Telescope, with Two Silicon Delta-E Detectors and a   O029100100044

            Energy Absorption. The Total Resolution was           O029100100046 
           Approximately 180 KeV For Most of the Data.            O029100100047 
           For the 61.5 MeV                                       O029100100048 
            Runs the Telescope was Shielded by a Tantalum or      O029100100049 
            Nickel Collimator with a Thickness of 0.432 and 0.653 O029100100050 
            Cm, Respectively. The Corresponding Areas were 0.183 -O029100100051 
            0.522 Cm2 +/- 1.5 %. At Some Angles, Also a 0.1       O029100100052 
            Cm Thick Ne201 Scintillator, with an Area of 0.353 Cm2O029100100053 
            +/- 1.5 %, was Used. For the Runs at 38.8 MeV         O029100100054 
            The Same Ne102 Collimator was Used. At 28.8 MeV a 0.13O029100100055 
            Cm Thick Tantalum Collimator, with an Area of 0.522   O029100100056 
            Cm2 +/- 1.5 %, was Used. The Distance from the        O029100100057 
            Target to the Collimator was 45.8 - 47.0 Cm +/- 1%.   O029100100058 
            The Collimator had a Misalignment at the Center       O029100100059 
            Of the Scattering Chamber of +/- 0.5 Cm. The PrecisionO029100100060 
            Of the Detector Angle was +/- 0.5 Degrees. The Zero   O029100100061 
            Angle was Determined to +/- 0.5 Degrees. The Angular  O029100100062 
            Resolution was +/- 1.2 Degrees.                       O029100100063 
SAMPLE     .Iron Target, 3.33 +/- 0.033 Mg/Cm2 Thick, with a      O029100100064
